      class=\"inline-share-btn inline-share-btn-more\"\n         data-share-method=\"facebook\"\n         data-uotrack=\"InlineShareMoreBtn\"><span class=\"inline-share-count inline-share-count-more\"></span><span class=\"inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-more\">MORE</span></span></div></div><p>INDIANAPOLIS (AP) \u2014 LeBron James finished with 41 points, 13 rebounds and 12 assists, and the Cleveland Cavaliers set an NBA postseason record by erasing a 25-point halftime deficit to beat the Indiana Pacers 119-114 on Thursday night and take a 3-0 lead.</p><p>James passed Kobe Bryant for No. 3 on the NBA's career playoff scoring list and tied another NBA record by winning his 20th consecutive first-round game.</p><p>The Cavaliers will try to sweep the series Sunday.</p><p>The incredible rally ruined Paul George's big night. He had 36 points, a playoff career-high 15 rebounds and nine assists.</p><p>Cleveland trailed by 26 in the first half and was still down 74-49 at halftime. The largest halftime deficit overcome to win a playoff game had been 21 points by Baltimore against Philadelphia in 1948.</p><div id=\"module-position-P5Fjr0GhIXY\" class=\"story-asset oembed-asset\"><div class=\"story-oembed-wrap \"><div \n        class=\"js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-sendtonews story-oembed-type-video\"\n        data-oembed-type=\"video\"\n        data-oembed-provider=\"sendtonews\"><div class='s2nPlayer-Hv4R35O75b-286289-5176' data-type='single'></div><script type='text/javascript' src='http://embed.sendtonews.com/player2/embedcode.php?SC=Hv4R35O75b-286289-5176' data-type='s2nScript'></script></div></div></div><p>James scored 13 points in the third quarter to get the Cavs within 91-84.</p><p>James now has 5,669 points, 29 ahead of Bryant. He also matched three other ex-Los Angeles Lakers \u2014 Magic Johnson, Michael Cooper and James Worthy \u2014 for most consecutive first-round wins.</p><p>This comeback began with a second straight devastating third-quarter punch from the Cavs.</p><p>After Cleveland cut the deficit to 77-62 and then watched Indiana extend the margin to 20, Cleveland finished the quarter on a 17-4 spurt to make it 91-84.</p><p>Things only got worse for the Pacers.</p><p>George's 3 with 5:15 to go gave Indiana a 104-103 lead \u2014 its last of the game. James answered with a layup out of a timeout and the Cavs never trailed again.</p><p><strong>MORE NBA:</strong></p><div id=\"module-position-P5Fjr0IPw_4\" class=\"story-asset oembed-asset\"><div class=\"story-oembed-wrap \"><div \n        class=\"js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-for-the-win story-oembed-type-link\"\n        data-oembed-type=\"link\"\n        data-oembed-provider=\"for-the-win\"><style>\n    .oembed-asset-link { border-bottom: 1px solid #e1e1e1; line-height: 120%; }\n</style><div class=\"oembed-asset oembed-asset-link oembed-asset-for-the-win oembed-simple-link-container\"><a href=\"http://ftw.usatoday.com/2017/04/myles-turner-destroyed-tristan-thompson-poster-dunk-video-cavaliers-pacers-nba-playoffs\" data-track-label=\"newrecircinline\" class=\"oembed-simple-link oembed-link-anchor\"><p class=\"oembed-link-desc\">Myles Turner destroyed Tristan Thompson with a jaw-dropping poster dunk</p><div style=\"clear: both;\"></div></a></div></div></div></div><div id=\"module-position-P5Fjr0JXHPM\" class=\"story-asset oembed-asset\"><div class=\"story-oembed-wrap \"><div \n        class=\"js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-usa-today story-oembed-type-link\"\n        data-oembed-type=\"link\"\n        data-oembed-provider=\"usa-today\"><style>\n    .oembed-asset-link { border-bottom: 1px solid #e1e1e1; $50M facility to merge sports, science</p><div style=\"clear: both;\"></div></a></div></div></div></div><p>It's only the second time in the Pacers' NBA history they have lost the first three games in a best-of-seven series. Indiana has never endured a four-game sweep since joining the NBA.</p><p><strong>TIP-INS: Cavaliers \u2014</strong>\u00a0Kyrie Irving Kevin Love, J.R. Smith, Channing Frye all scored 13 points. ... Cleveland has won six straight over Indiana. ... After scoring 49 points in the first half, the Cavs scored 35 in each of the final two quarters. ... Kyle Korver scored more points in two quarters (six) than he did in the first two games (four). He finished with 12.</p><p><strong>Pacers \u2014</strong>\u00a0George had 23 points, nine rebounds and five assists, and Lance Stephenson added eight points and five rebounds in the first two quarters. ... Indiana scored 37 points in the first quarter, falling just short of a season high (39), then matched that 37 in the second quarter for its highest first-half total of the season. ... Coach Nate McMillan made a lineup change, inserting former Cavs player C.J. Miles into the starting rotation. Monta Ellis was relegated to bench duty. ... The Pacers drew two defensive three-second calls in the first half.</p><p><strong>UP NEXT:</strong> On Sunday, Indiana will try to stave off elimination when it hosts Cleveland for Game 4.</p><div "url": "https://www.usatoday.com/story/sports/nba/2017/04/20/james-cavs-come-from-26-down-beat-pacers-to-take-3-0-lead/100728802/", "date": "04-20-2017", "source": "usa-today", "text": "CLOSE Skip in Skip x Embed x Share The Cavaliers erased a 25-point halftime lead to beat the Pacers and take a 3-0 lead in the series.\n\nLeBron James' 17th career playoff triple-double led the Cavs' to an historic comeback. (Photo: Brian Spurlock, USA TODAY Sports)\n\nINDIANAPOLIS (AP) \u2014 LeBron James finished with 41 points, 13 rebounds and 12 assists, and the Cleveland Cavaliers set an NBA postseason record by erasing a 25-point halftime deficit to beat the Indiana Pacers 119-114 on Thursday night and take a 3-0 lead.\n\nJames passed Kobe Bryant for No. 3 on the NBA's career playoff scoring list and tied another NBA record by winning his 20th consecutive first-round game.\n\nThe Cavaliers will try to sweep the series Sunday.\n\nThe incredible rally ruined Paul George's big night. He had 36 points, a playoff career-high 15 rebounds and nine assists.\n\nCleveland trailed by 26 in the first half and was still down 74-49 at halftime. The largest halftime deficit overcome to win a playoff game had been 21 points by Baltimore against Philadelphia in 1948.\n\nJames scored 13 points in the third quarter to get the Cavs within 91-84.\n\nJames now has 5,669 points, 29 ahead of Bryant. He also matched three other ex-Los Angeles Lakers \u2014 Magic Johnson, Michael Cooper and James Worthy \u2014 for most consecutive first-round wins.\n\nThis comeback began with a second straight devastating third-quarter punch from the Cavs.\n\nAfter Cleveland cut the deficit to 77-62 and then watched Indiana extend the margin to 20, Cleveland finished the quarter on a 17-4 spurt to make it 91-84.\n\nThings only got worse for the Pacers.\n\nGeorge's 3 with 5:15 to go gave Indiana a 104-103 lead \u2014 its last of the game. James answered with a layup out of a timeout and the Cavs never trailed again.\n\nMORE NBA:\n\nIt's only the second time in the Pacers' NBA history they have lost the first three games in a best-of-seven series. Indiana has never endured a four-game sweep since joining the NBA.\n\nTIP-INS: Cavaliers \u2014 Kyrie Irving Kevin Love, J.R. Smith, Channing Frye all scored 13 points. ... Cleveland has won six straight over Indiana. ... After scoring 49 points in the first half, the Cavs scored 35 in each of the final two quarters. ... Kyle Korver scored more points in two quarters (six) than he did in the first two games (four). He finished with 12.\n\nPacers \u2014 George had 23 points, nine rebounds and five assists, and Lance Stephenson added eight points and five rebounds in the first two quarters. ... Indiana scored 37 points in the first quarter, falling just short of a season high (39), then matched that 37 in the second quarter for its highest first-half total of the season. ... Coach Nate McMillan made a lineup change, inserting former Cavs player C.J. Miles into the starting rotation. Monta Ellis was relegated to bench duty. ... The Pacers drew two defensive three-second calls in the first half.\n\nUP NEXT: On Sunday, Indiana will try to stave off elimination when it hosts Cleveland for Game 4.\n\nCopyright 2017 The Associated Press. All rights reserved.
